# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="92ad1-103">Cadeias de criptografia do Microsoft 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ad1-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92ad1-104">O Microsoft 365 aproveita vários provedores de certificados diferentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ad1-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92ad1-105">O exemplo a seguir descreve a lista completa de certificados raiz conhecidos do Microsoft 365 que os clientes podem encontrar ao acessar o Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ad1-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92ad1-106">Para obter informações sobre os certificados que talvez você precise instalar em sua própria infraestrutura, consulte Planejar certificados SSL de terceiros para [o Microsoft 365.](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ad1-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="92ad1-107">As informações de certificado a seguir se aplica a todas as instâncias de nuvem nacional e mundial do Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ad1-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="92ad1-108">Last updated: **16/10/2020**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ad1-108">Last updated: **10/16/2020**</span></span>
